<p><a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>noun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> derived <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:late.html>Late</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:nik.html>nik</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">notch, <a href = vnd.unilang:tally.html>tally</a>; <p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nieman</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">nieman</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">n-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieten.html>nieten</a> (68503)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nieten.html>nieten</a></strong>
</p>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">nyghtyngale</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">niȝtingale</i>, alteration (<a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> intrusive <i>n</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">nyghtgale</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">nightegale</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">nihtegala</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">nihtegale</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a>; <hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">nightingales</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:european.html>European</a> songbird, <i>Luscinia megarhynchos</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:family.html>family</a> Muscicapidae.
<ul><li><b>1826</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mary_Shelley" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mary Shelley"><a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> Shelley</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:chapter.html>chapter</a> 5 <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:first.html>first</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:part.html>part</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Last_Man" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Last Man"><a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:last.html>Last</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a></a></i>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oaks.html>oaks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:around.html>around</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:home.html>home</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tribe.html>tribe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <b>nightingales</b></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>Nightingales</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:have.html>have</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> spotted <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>this</a> coppice.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:you.html>You</a> sing <a href = vnd.unilang:like.html>like</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:nightingale.html>nightingale</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sport.html>sport</a>!</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***nihilisme.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nihilisme.html>nihilisme</a> (74065)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Nihilismus</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:itself.html>itself</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:nihil.html>nihil</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:nil.html>nil</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:nothing.html>nothing</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a> -ismus '-ism', coined <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> 1817 <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:philosopher.html>philosopher</a> Friedrich Heinrich Jacobi, <a href = vnd.unilang:but.html>but</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:repeatedly.html>repeatedly</a> 'reinvented'.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nihilisme.html>nihilisme</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nihilisme.html>nihilismes</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nihilisme.html>nihilismes</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nihilisme.html>nihilismethe</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
